Et aucune fois dessent li cirbes avec l’intestine, et est retenus enqui, et fait grant dolor soffrir au malaide, meismement quant il est pressez.	 And sometimes the rings go with the intestines, and are retained therein, causing great pain for the patient, especially when pressed.
Et en ces cures de fer a paor, por coi il s’en covient eschuir.	 And in these cauterizations with iron, because of fear, one must avoid them.
Et li maniere de l’ovraige si est que tu comande ou malaide qu’il ramoine l’intestine a sa main au dedens en la plaie, s’il i puet rentreir;	 And the manner of the work is such that you instruct the patient to pull out the intestines with his hand within the wound, if he can reach.
puis soit sovinez sus son col. entre tes mains, et lieve les cuixes;	 then support him on his neck, between your hands, and lift the thighs;
puis estent le keur au desus, et cope tout le cuir des coions dou lonc;	 then press the heart downwards, and cut all the skin of the testicles from top to bottom.
puis boute dedens les leivres de la taille uncines selonc ceu que tu en as mestier por ovrir la plaie, et soit telz que li oes em puist issir;	 then push inside the intestines of the belly some hooks according to what you need to open the wound, and let it be such that the feces may exit.
puis escorche lou syfac que est desoz lou cuir des coions, tant que li blans syfac dur soit descovers de toutes pars;	 then remove the fat that is under the skin of the testicles, so that all parts of the hard white fat are exposed.
puis boute ton doi indice en ceu qui enseut lou coion, en ceu qui est entre lou blanc syfac qui est desoz lou cuir de l’uef, et entre lou secont syfac, et depart ceu qui est derrier l’uef, et entre lou secont syfac;	 then insert your finger into that which follows the testicle, in that which is between the white fat under the skin of the egg, and between the second fat layer, and separate what is behind the egg, and between the second fat layer.
et pues muef a la main destre dedens lou keur des coions, et estent lou blanc syfac en haut a ta main senestre, et lieve l’uef a tout lou syfac devers la taille;	 And then move to the right hand inside the heart of the kidneys, and extend the white silk up to your left hand, and lift the egg towards the waist with all the silk.
et comande au ministre qu’il estende l’uef en haut, et deslie ceu qui est aers derrier le liement;	 And instruct the assistant to extend the egg upward, and untie what is tied behind the binding.
et quier a tes dois s’il a point de l’intestine envoloupeit ou blanc syfac dur, et se tu en trueves aucune chose, si le boute au ventre desoz;	 And ask your two assistants if there is any part of the intestine wrapped in hard white silk, and if you find anything, push it down into the stomach.
puis pren une aguille ou il ait I gros fil fait de X filz, et la boute en la derriere partie dou syfac, qui est aprés lou cuir des coions;	 Then take a needle with a thread made of ten threads, and push it into the rear part of the silk, which is behind the skin of the kidneys.
aprés la taille, puis cope les chiés qui apperent des filz, tant qu’il i ait IIII filz;	 After the waist, then cut the threads that appear from the needles, until there are four threads.
puis les assemble l’un sus l’autre en maniere de croix, et en lie lou syfac, dont nos avons dit qui est desoz lou cuir des coions, d’un fort liien de II pars;	 Then assemble them one on top of the other in the manner of a cross, and tie them with a strong cord of two parts;
puis envoloupe les chiés des filz, et les lie forment de II pars, si que nuls des vasselz que les norrissent ne puissent entrer en ous, que aposteme chaus n’i viegne;	 Then wrap the heads with thread, and tie them firmly with two parts, so that no creature that nurses them can enter inside, lest an abscess form there;
et met derechief le liien selonc le premier liien lonc II dois de celui, et aprés ces II liiens laisse dou syfac qui est desoz lou keur des coions le grant d’un doi;	 And put the cord back in place according to the first long cord, and after these two cords leave a piece of the thread that is under the skin of the knees the width of a finger;
et aprés tout l’autre selonc la rondesce que li euf porte;	 And then all the rest according to the roundness that the egg bears;
puis cope en la partie qui est desoz le cuir des coions, tant qui li sans corre, et li bowe, si com nos avons dit ci devant;	 Then cut in the part that is under the skin of the knees until the blood runs and boils, as we have said before;
puis amenistre laine moillie en oile, et met em plaies, et i amenistre le liien que nos avons dit.	 Then introduce wet wool soaked in oil, and place it on the wounds, and there introduce the bandage that we have mentioned.
Et aucune fois est cauterizez li blans syfac que nos avons dit, aprés l’incision, par doutance de decorrement de sanc.	 And sometimes the white flesh is cauterized as we have said, after the incision, out of fear of bleeding.
Car ce avient maintes fois, et laisse le liien tant qu’il chiece per lui;	 For this happens often, and leave the bandage until it falls off by itself;
et s’il tarde au cheoir, si soit arosez d’aigue chaude, et met sus ceu que nos avons dit, tant qu’il chiece;	 and if it is slow to fall off, then wash it with hot water, and place (it) on that which we have said, until it falls off;
puis cure la plaie d’autre cure, tant qu’il soit sanez parfaitement.	 then treat the wound with another treatment, until it is perfectly healed.
de hernie carnouse	 of flesh hernia
En ceste ramice ne vis je onques nul qui osast faire la cure par fer.	 In this branch, I have never seen anyone who dared to make the cut with iron.
Et li ancien dirent qu’ele est faite si com li ramice qui est ensamble la vis, en teil maniere que tu lie les vasselz, aprés la taille sus ous legierement au desoz;	 And the ancients said that it is done as with the string that is with the screw, in such a way that you tie the vessels, after cutting slightly above and below;
puis cope em mi, et cure l’aposteme de ceu qui oevre, tant que li vasselz chient;	 then cut in half, and treat the abscess with that which works, until the vessel falls out;
et le cure si com nos avons dit, tant qu’il soit sanez.	 And let the treatment be as we have said, until he is healed.
Aucune fois vient routure ens angres, si com nos avons dit, et apert li leus;	 Sometimes there is fracturing in joints, as we have said, and the place opens;
et ne dessent nulz des intestines as coions, et s’il en i dessent, c’est poc, et repaire toutes houres;	 And no one should discharge from the intestines like dogs, and if they do, it is little, and it closes up every hour.
et toutevoie s’il demoure trop en cest point, si croit li plaie ou syphac, tant que li intestine dessent;	 Yet if it remains too long in this state, the wound or ulcer grows until the intestines discharge.
et ceu avient par l’estension dou syfac qui est as angres, si com nos avons dit, car il est estendus, puis est mollifiez et enflez li leus et apert;	 And this happens due to the extension of the ulcer that is in the joints, as we have said, for it becomes extended and the place is softened and swollen and open.
et li cure si est par cautere, si com nos avons devant dit;	 And the treatment is by cautery, as we have said before.
et aucune fois est curee par fer en ceste maniere:	 And sometimes it is treated with iron in this manner:
et est que li malaides gise sovin sus son dos entre tes mains, puis cope le leu de la routure enfleit dou large selonc la quantiteit de III dois;	 and the patient should lie on their back between your hands, then strike the swollen area with a broad blade according to the size of three fingers;
et puis estrai le syfac qui est desoz le cuir que l’ensuet, puis pren lou rait et lou met sor le leu apparant dou syfac;	 and then extract the pus that is beneath the skin with a hook, then take the cautery iron and place it on the visible part of the wound;
et lou presse au parfont dou ventre, puis cout les II leus apparans dou syfac sus lou chief dou rait, et cout l’un et l’autre;	 and press firmly with your hand, then place the cautery iron on the two visible parts of the wound on top of the hook, and burn both places;
puis estrai le chief dou rait, et ne coper point dou syfac ne n’estendre l’uef n’autre chose, si com je t’ai fait savoir en la cure de la ramice des intestines;	 then remove the cautery iron and do not cut the wound or spread any ointment or other substance, as I have taught you in the treatment of intestinal rupture;
puis le cure par la cure des plaies.	 Then the treatment by treating the wounds.
Et quant tu copes les filz, si le mundefie et cure la plaie, tant qu’elle soit sanee.	 And when you cut the threads, clean and treat the wound until it is healed.
Li syfac est constrains, et n’a point d’apparance en la routure, et li cauteres est muedres en cest leu, et plus prochiens a salut.	 The incision is tight, and has no appearance in the suture, and the cautery is better in this place, and closer to healing.
de l’amollissement dou cuir des coions	 of the softening of the skin of the testicles
Maintes fois est amollis li cuirs des coions en aucuns homes, por ceu que les chars que sont dedens sont mollifiees, et est lait a veoir;	 Many times the skin of the testicles in some men is softened because the glands within are softened, and this is evident to see.
et est mestier, quant on le vuet curer, c’on faice gesir lou malaide sus son dos, et li cope le cuir qui est mollifiez sus le cuir natureil;	 and it is necessary that when one wants to cure it, the patient lies on his back, and one cuts the softened skin onto the natural skin;
puis assemble les II levres a une costure, et se tu vues, cout premier la superfluiteit dou cuir mollifiiez a III costures ou IIII fermement;	 then sew together the two lips in one stitch, and if you wish, first sew down the excess skin with three or four strong stitches.
puis cope entre les costures, et lou cure si com les autres plaies, tant qu’il soit sanez, et chient li fil.	 then cut between the stitches, and treat it as you would other wounds until it is healed, and the threads fall out.
dou chastrement	 Of the castration
Saiches que chastremens est escomeniez en nostre loi, et por ceu il me plairoit que je n’en parlasse mie en cest livre;	 Know that castration is considered a disgrace in our law, and therefore I would prefer not to speak of it in this book.
et n’est necessaires fuer que por II manieres:	 And there are necessary for two ways:
dont l’une est que li mires en saiche respondre quant on li demandera, et en saiche la cure;	 which is one of them that the physician knows how to answer when asked, and knows the cure;
et li autre, por ceu que nos avons sovent mestier de chastrement d’aucunes bestes por nos aidier, si com de bouc et de mouton et de chait et d’autres bestes.	 and the other is because we often have need of castration of some animals to help us, such as goats and sheep and dogs and other animals.
Je dis donques que chastremens est fais selonc II manieres:	 Therefore, I say that castration is done in two ways:
ou par atraction, ou par fendure.	 either by attraction or by cutting.
En celle que nos faisons par attraction, faisons nos seoir la beste en aigue chaude, tant que li coion soient mollifiez et pendant;	 In that which we do by attraction, we make the animal sit in hot water until its testicles are softened and hanging;
puis les preing a ta main, tant qu’il soient remis et que tu ne les sentes plus.	 then take them in your hand until they are retracted and you no longer feel them.
Du chastrement de taille:	 Of castration by cutting:
covient que tu teignes la beste, et li presse le cuir des coions a ta main senestre, puis lie le suspensoire, et cope sus chescun oef a I cop, quant tu les avras bien escorchiez;	 It is necessary that you dye the beast, and press the skin of the testicles to your left hand, then tie the suspensory ligament, and cut on each testicle with one stroke, when you have well scraped them;
et i laisse aucun poc dou syfac et lou subtil syfac qui est sor les vasselz;	 and leave any pouch of the scrotum and the fine scrotum that is on the vessels;
et ceste maniere de chastrement est muedre que cele qui est faite par attraction, por ceu que a l’atraction demoure par aventure aucune chose des coions, par coi li beste desire luxure;	 and this method of castration is better than that done by attraction, because in the case of attraction, there may remain something from the testicles, which causes the beast to desire lust.
puis cure la plaie tant qu’ele soit sanee.	 then heal the wound until it is healed.
des hermofrodites	 et li presse le cuir des coions a ta main senestre
Hermofrodie est selonc II manieres as homes:	 Hermaphroditism occurs in two ways in men:
l’une si est que entre les II coions apert ausi com li figure de la nature d’une femme, ou il ait poil, et aucunes fois en cort li urine.	 one way is that between the two testicles there appears as if by the design of nature like a woman, where there is hair, and sometimes urine flows from it.
Et li autre maniere si est en femmes, et ait sus lou poignil ausi com une verge et II coions.	 Et tels estre ne puet avoir en nule manere d’enfanz: quar il ne poet pas faire l’un ne l’autre office de sa nature.
Et li cure de l’ome et de la fame si est que tu copes les chars ajostees toutes, et les cure si com autres plaies;	 And the cure of a man and a woman is such that you cut all the flesh close together, and treat it as other wounds.
en la seconde maniere, des homes dont li urine saut par lou cuir des coions, si n’a point de cure.	 in the second manner, of the men whose urine comes out through the skin of the testicles, there is no cure.
de la tentigene	 of venereal disease
Tentigene est une chars ajostee sus la partie natureil, tant qu’elle est trop laide a veoir;	 A tumor is flesh that has grown on the natural part, until it becomes very ugly to see;
et aucunes femmes l’ont ausi grant com une main, et c’est li cure.	 and some women have it as large as a hand, and this is the treatment.
Il covient que tu teignes la superfluiteit de la tentigene a ta main ou as oncines, et la cope legierement;	 It is necessary that you cut away the excess of the tumor with your hand or with scissors, and cut it lightly;
et n’aler mie trop em parfont, que decorremens de sanc n’i viegne, puis le cure d’autre cure tant qu’il soit sanez;	 and do not go too deep, so that blood does not come out, then treat it with another treatment until it is healed.
et a une autre char que naist a la bouche de la marris, et l’emple, et par aventure saut fuer, et est selonc la semblance d’une kowe, et por ceu l’apelerent li ancien «maladie kowee».	 And to another wound that forms at the mouth of the uterus, and fills it, and perhaps jumps forth, and is according to the appearance of a cow, and for this reason the ancients called it "cow disease".
Si covient que tu la copes, si com nos avons dit la tentigene, et la cure tant qu’elle soit sanee.	 If necessary, you must cut it, as we have said regarding the tendon, and treat it until it is healed.
de erratique	 of the dislocated
Erratique si est quant li nature de la femme n’est mie percie, ou li pertus est petis;	 It occurs when the woman's nature is not clear, or the opening is small.
et est naturez par naissance, ou accidens par maladie que venue i est;	 and it is caused either by birth, or by accident due to a disease that has come upon her.
ou c’est par char ajostee, ou dou syfac subtil ou espés, et est fais em parfont en la marris, ou en costez, ou desoz, ou que soit;	 or it is caused by a deep wound, or by a subtle or thick secretion, and it is formed deep within the uterus, or on its sides, or beneath it, wherever it may be.
et deffent le concevoir, et l’enfantement, et par aventure les flors a avoir;	 and prevents conception, and childbirth, and perhaps even menstruation.
et li connoissance de ceu si est par le regart de la baile.	 And the recognition of this is by the gaze of the wound.
Se li estoupemens est prochiens apparans, si quier a tes dois ou au rait.	 If the blindness seems imminent, let it be near your hands or feet.
S’il est dou syfac subtil, et il est prochiens as II leivres, si te haste, et la ront ensi:	 If it is subtle in color and is near two pounds, hasten, and do thus:
met tes II dois indices ensamble, et li femme soit sus son dos, espandues ses jambes;	 Place your two fingers together, and have the woman lie on her back with her legs spread;
puis estent les II leivres forment, tant que li subtilz syfac soit rons, et soit overs li estoupemens;	 then weigh out the two pounds firmly until the subtle color is gone, and the swelling has passed.
puis pren laine, et la moille en oile, et la met sus le leu, et gise li femme a home chescun jor, si qu’il ne puist souder.	 Then take wool, and soak it in oil, and place it on the spot, and have the woman lie down every day so that it cannot close.
Et se li syfac est dur et espés, si covient que tu lou copes au spatumile semblant a foille de mirte.	 And if the syphilis is hard and thick, you must cut it with a scalpel similar to a myrtle leaf blade.
Se li estoupemens est de char nee, si la sospent a l’oncine et la cope;	 If the swelling is of flesh and bone, then suspend it with an onion and cut it;
et aies les medicines estainchans sanc, si com acaice, sanc de dragon, encens, ensamble abun d’uef;	 And have the medicines that staunch blood, such as acacia, dragon's blood, incense, together with plenty of egg.
puis amenistre une caine de plonc large, si que li plaie ne puisse souder;	 then bring a wide lead spoon, so that the wound cannot close
et ensi soit longement, et li amenistre une tente de lin sec;	 and let it be thus for a long time, and bring him a tent of dry linen
puis soit curez d’autres cures tant qu’il soit sanez.	 then let him be treated with other treatments until he is healed.
Et quant en la marris vient char nee, si la covient coper selonc ceste maniere, se ce n’est apostemes enchancrez.	 And when a char is born into the womb, it must be covered in this manner, unless it is an encrusted abscess.
Car a l’aposteme enchancreit qui est en la marris, ne doit on touchier de feir.	 For the encrusted abscess that is in the womb, one should not touch or make fire.
des emorroides	 of hemorrhoids
Emorroydes sont overtures de voines dont sans cort acostumeement, et quant les emorroydes sont vielles si devienent thelul;	 Hemorrhoids are openings of veins which, without a covering, are usually exposed, and when hemorrhoids are old, they become hard.
et nos avons jai dit en la division les semblances d’aus, et les signes, et je dirai ci celles qui resoivent curation.	 and we have already said in the division their appearance, and the signs, and I will say here those which receive treatment.
Je di que les emorroides et li thelul, quant il sont em parfont en la marris, et il n’aperent au sentir, si n’est mie li cure par fer.	 I say that hemorrhoids and the hardened ones, when they are deep in the womb and do not appear to be felt, then treatment by fire is not appropriate.
Cil qui sont a la bouche de la marris, c’on puet sentir, sont cil c’on puet curer.	 Those who are at the mouth of the wound, where one can feel them, are those that can be healed.
Il covient donques que tu mettes la femme en une maison froide, puis estent l’altelul as tenailles, et le cope en ses racines, puis poudre sus medicines restraignans sanc, si com acaice et sanc de dragon et encens, et semblans choses;	 Therefore, you must place the woman in a cold house, then cauterize with tongs, and cut out its roots, then sprinkle on powdered hemostatic medicines such as vinegar, dragon's blood, and incense, and similar things.
puis boute ses piez a la paroit une houre, puis la met en aigue froide;	 Then make him put his feet against the wall for an hour, then put them in cold water.
et se decorremens de sanc i vient, si la fai seoir en une decoction de sumac et d’escorce de pomes grenates et de gales et de semblans choses, et puis pren farine d’orge, et la confis avec miel et aisil, et en fai I emplaustre sus son dos.	 And if blood continues to flow from there, then make her sit in a decoction of sumac and apple tree bark, and galls and similar things, and then take barley flour, and mix it with honey and vinegar, and make a poultice on her back with it.
Et se il estainche, c’est boin.	 And if it festers, it is good.
Se ceu non, se li fai aerdre ventouses au dos et as mameles sens ferir;	 If not, then let air out through cupping glasses on the back and breasts without pricking;
puis pren lainne, et la moille en jus de plantain ou en jus d’aglentier avec vin viel, et fai aerdre au leu.	 Then take wool, and soak it in plantain juice or hawthorn juice with old wine, and let it out in that place.
Et quant li aposteme repose, si cure lou leu d’oignement tant qu’il soit sanez;	 And when the abscess has subsided, then treat the place with onion oil until it is healed.
et celle qui est apelee «albathir» est rouge, et est semblans a I chief aspre, si le covient coper si com j’ai dit le thelul;	 And that which is called "albathir" is red, and it resembles the sharp point, so you must cover it as I have said for the telul.
et puis lou cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	 And then let the wound heal until it is healed.
des apostemes de la marris	 of the abscesses of the shin
Maintes manieres d’aposteme vienent en la marris, si com chancre et aposteme pierous et herpes et estiomenes et fistules et emorroides et aposteme chaut, et plusors autres maladies que j’ai dit en la division.	 Many kinds of abscess come to the shin, such as chancre and piercing abscess and herpes and carbuncles and fistulas and hemorrhoids and hot abscess, and many other diseases that I have mentioned in the division.
Il covient donques que je die en cest traitier l’aposteme chaut qui vient en la marris, qui n’est mie des apostemes que coillent bowe;	 Therefore, I must say in this treatise about the hot abscess that comes on the back, which is not one of the abscesses that grow big;
et se tu vues savoir l’ovraige de fer, si regarde se li apostemes est agus en l’encomencement de sa venue, et plain de chalor et de fievre, et s’il devient rouge se tu le pues veoir.	 and if you want to know the work of iron, then consider whether the abscess is acute at the beginning of its appearance, and full of heat and fever, and whether it turns red if you can see it.
Adonques ne te haster mie de percier, mais lou fais meurer tant que li dolor soit apaisie;	 Then do not hasten to pierce, but let the abscess ripen until the pain is relieved;
et puis fai seoir lou malaide sus I siege, et ait II petis sieges ou il se cline, et apoie sus son dos et assemble ses piez as parties defuer la jambe;	 And then have the patient sit on the seat, and let there be two small seats where he leans back, and supports his back and gathers his feet together outside the leg.
et soient ses cuixes espandues, et mette ses braz desoz ses genous, et les lie bien d’un boin liien;	 And let his thighs be spread wide, and place his arms under his knees, and bind them well with a good ligature.
puis succe li baille devers lou destre costeit, et i amenistre l’estrument dont on oevre la bouche de la marris, de coi ci aprés vient li forme;	 Then give the patient something to drink towards his right side, and bring the instrument with which one opens the mouth of the wound, from which then comes the shape.
et covient que quant tu i vues amenistrer cest estrument, que tu fiches le rait premier ens por savoir la parfondeté de la marris, si que ceu qui entre ens de l’estrument n’i viegne plus em parfont qu’il ne doit, et qu’il ne blece la malaide;	 And it is necessary that when you see the instrument being brought near, that you first insert a reed to know the depth of the wound, so that what enters from the instrument does not go deeper than it should, and does not harm the patient.
et se li estrumens est plus grans, si covient covrir la parfondesce de la marris de drapelz, si que li estrumens ne li grieve;	 And if the instrument is too large, it must be covered with cloths to prevent it from hurting.
et covient qu’il mette le cornet de l’estrument au desus, et qu’il teigne l’estrument.	 And he must put the horn of the instrument on top and dip the instrument.
Et quant li apostemes apert, et on lou fent a la main mol, si le covient coper au chief, au spatumile leit;	 And when the abscess opens and one makes an opening in the soft part of the hand, it must be covered at the top with spathe milk.
et quant li bowe est vuidie, si covient que tu mettes en la plaie tentes moillies en oile roset, ou en oile vert sec;	 And when the wound is emptied, then you must put moist linen cloths in rose oil or in dry green oil into the wound.
et met la tente fuer de la plaie au parfont de la marris, et met par defuer sus la marris et sus le poignil lainne nette moillie en aigue ou malves soient cuites;	 And place the edge of the cloth inside the wound at the bottom of the flesh, and place another on top of the flesh and on the joint clean linen moistened in boiled water or mallow.
puis le cure aprés II jors d’oignement avenant a ceu, tant qu’il soit sanez;	 Then the treatment after two days of soaking, as long as it is healed;
et aucune fois leve on la marris et la plaie par clistere d’aigue et de miel, et puis d’aigue ou racines de lis et aristologe longe soient cuites;	 and sometimes the scab and the wound are lifted by an enema of water and honey, and then with water and roots of lily and long-stemmed plants that have been cooked;
puis reveigne a l’oignement.	 then it returns to soaking.
Et se li plaie est reponue en la marris, si covient que tu te gardes de cuire de fer, mais cure la si com nos avons dit en la division.	 And if the wound is festering in the marrow, then you must be careful not to burn with iron, but heal it as we have said in the division.
de l’enfantement	 of childbirth
Mestier est premier a la baile qu’elle conoisse la figure de l’enfantement natureil, et li signes si est quant tu vois la femme apresser aval, et desire odorer l’ar:	 It is necessary for the midwife to first know the natural process of childbirth, and the signs are when you see the woman pushing downwards, and desiring to smell the air:
adonques se haste li enfes de fuer issir;	 then the child hastens to exit by force.
adonc saiches que cil enfantemens est selonc la figure natureil, et est li issue soz son chief, et li secondine avec lui;	 then know that this birth is according to the natural process, and the exit is under its head, and the afterbirth with it.
et quant tu vois ces signes, si covient presser legierement son ventre, si que li enfes isse tost;	 And when you see these signs, then it is necessary to gently press on his belly, so that the child comes out quickly;
car quant il dessent sus son chief, si ist li secondine avec lui, et est mondee li marris de ses superfluitez par bone mundification;	 for when he descends onto his head, then the placenta comes with him, and the mother is cleansed of her excesses by a good cleaning;
et cist qui vient autrement ne vient mie naturelment.	 and those who come otherwise do not come naturally.
Car il vient aucune fois sus ses piez, et vient fuer li cors ou li chiés, et les mains, ou il vient sus son ventre, ou sovin, et est convertis par aventure sor son col, et par autres figures malvaises;	 For sometimes he comes on his feet, and sometimes he comes out violently through the body or the head, and the hands, or he comes on his belly, or sometimes, and he is turned by chance onto his neck, and in other bad forms;
si est mestier a la baile qu’elle soit saige et subtilz en ces choses, et se warse d’error et de decevement, et je vos mostrerai toutes les figures coment on li doit aidier.	 it is necessary for the midwife that she be wise and skilled in these things, and beware of error and deceit, and I will show you all the forms in which one must assist her.
Se li enfes vient sus son chief par issue natureil, et li femme enfante griement, et li vertus de li est foible, si la fai seoir sus une selle, ou les femmes la tienent;	 Se the child comes out of its head by natural birth, and the woman gives birth in pain, and the child's strength is weak, then have her sit on a saddle, where the women hold her;
et arose sa nature d’oile ou fenugreic soit cuit, et puis boute li baile entre ses dois le petit spatumile dont ci est li forme:	 and let its nature be of oil or fenugreek, which has been cooked, and then pour the bath between her teeth a little spoonful of which the form is here:
et fende la secondine, et cope a son ungle tant que li moistors qui est ens corre fuers;	 and cut the afterbirth, and scrape off at her fingernail until the moisture that is within runs out;
et preint lou ventre de la femme tant que li enfes dessende, et s’il ne dessent, si covient clisterizer la femme de muscillaige de fenugrec avec oile de sisament;	 and press the woman's belly until the child descends, and if it does not descend, then it is necessary to give the woman a clyster of fenugreek mustard with sesame oil;
puis la fai preindre et esternuer de condisi, et tien sa bouche et son neis une houre:	 then have her take and sneeze pepper, and hold her mouth and nose for an hour:
si istra maintenant l’enfes.	 If one extracts the child now.
Et se les II mains issent fuer, si covient que tu les ramoinne legierement poc et poc;	 And if both hands come out forcibly, then you must reset them lightly bit by bit;
et s’elles n’i puent entrer, si met la femme sus I siege, et li lieve les piés en haut;	 and if they cannot go back in, then place the woman on a stool, and lift her feet up high;
puis deboute le siege sus terre, et teigne on la femme, qu’elle ne chiece au deboutement;	 then knock the stool over onto the ground, and hold the woman so that she does not fall during the toppling.
et se li mains n’i puet entrer, et li enfes muert, si li cope les mains au couteil qui est ci devant mis, et estrai l’enfant, et ramoine igalment.	 and if the hand cannot go back in and the child dies, then cut off the hands with the knife that was placed here before, and extract the child, and reset it likewise.
de l’issue de l’enfant sus ses piés	 of the child’s birth on its feet
Quant li enfes vient sus ses piez, si lou covient bouter en haut;	 When the child comes out on its feet, one must push it upwards;
et puis le torne poc et poc, tant qu’il soit igalz;	 and then turn it bit by bit until it is even.
puis preigne I des piez et l’estende poc et poc.	 Then take a hold of one foot and extend it little by little.
Cant il saut jusc’as cuixes, si la comande a preindre, et la fai esternuer de condisi;	 When he can jump to his knees, then instruct him to grasp it, and make it sneeze conditionally;
si saut fuer, se Deus vuet.	 if he jumps farther, God willing.
Et s’il n’ist fuer si com nos avons dit, si le torne poc et poc, tant qu’il soit selonc la figure natureil.	 And if he does not jump as we have said, then turn him little by little until he is according to the natural figure.
Car adonques ist il legierement.	 For then it is easily done.
Et s’il ne vient fuer si com nos avons, dit si pren muscillaige de altee, et oile de sisament, et gomme fondue, et broie tout en I mortier;	 And if he does not come farther as we have said, then take mullein of hart's-tongue, and oil of balsam, and melted gum, and grind all in a mortar;
et met sus la nature de la femme dedens et defuer cest oignement, puis la fai seoir en aigue tede jusque desoz les costelz;	 and place this ointment on the woman's genitalia inside and outside, then make her sit in hot water up to the ribs.
et quant elle est moillifie desoz, se li fai I coliere de mirre, et li met desoz, et li laisse une houre;	 And when she is well soaked beneath, give her a potion of myrrh, and place it beneath, and leave it there for an hour.
puis la fai seoir sus I siege, puis la fai esternuer et estraint sa bouche et son neis, et li preint le ventre legierement, car li enfes saut maintenant.	 then have her sit on the seat, then make her sneeze and hold her mouth and nose, and gently press her belly, for the child is about to jump out now.
de l’issue de l’enfant sus ses genous	 of the child's exit on its knees
Quant li enfes vient en ceste forme, si i mette li baile ses mains poc et poc;	 When the child comes in this manner, then have the midwife place her hands little by little;
puis soit sovinee sus son col, et li pendent li piez aval, et soit gisans sor I lit;	 then have her sit back on her heels, and let her feet hang down, and she should lie on the bed.
et plie ses mains poc et poc, et puis li preint les mains sus lou ventre, et li oste les cussins desoz, tant qu’elle soit appareillie aval;	 and let her bend her hands little by little, and then have her place her hands on the belly, and remove the cushions from beneath, so that she is prepared below.
et se li enfes ne saut, si pren ses piez et li muef forment, puis li muef lou ventre amont, puis i boute tes mains;	 And if the child does not jump out, take her feet and move them strongly, then move the belly upwards, then push with your hands.
et ewe l’enfant poc et poc;	 And give the child little by little;
et comande a la femme qu’elle se preigne tant que li enfes isse.	 and instruct the woman to take hold of herself until the child comes out.
de l’issue de l’enfant qui vient dou large une main pendant	 of the issue of the child which comes from a wide hand hanging
I covient engignier a ramener la main:	 It is necessary to contrive to bring back the hand:
s’on ne la puet ramener, si fai lever la femme, et aler;	 if it cannot be brought back, then lift up the woman and let her walk.
s’elle ne puet aler, si la fai gesir sus I lit, et li deboute les jambes forment;	 if she cannot walk, then make her lie on a bed and spread her legs wide.
puis amenistre lou muscillaige que j’ai conteit;	 then apply the instrument that I have described.
et s’elle n’enfante, si la fai seoir sus I siege, puis estudie au rameneir la main;	 and if she does not give birth, then make her sit on a stool, then study to bring back the hand.
et ewe l’enfant selonc la figure natureil, et la fai esternuer, et li comande qu’elle se preigne tant que li enfes isse fuer.	 and give the child according to its natural form, and make it sneeze, and instruct her to take hold of herself until the child comes out strongly.
de l’issue de l’enfant sus son col, et ait espandues ses mains, et sa faice tornee devers lou dos sa mere	 of the issue of the child on its neck, and with hands spread out, and face turned towards the back of its mother.
I covient que li baile teigne sa main, puis le torne poc et poc, et l’ewe legierement;	 It is necessary that the patient keep their hand still, then turn it a little at a time, and move it gently.
et quant il est igalz, si met sus la nature muscillaige de altee et oile, si com nos avons dit, puis li comande qu’elle se mueve poc et poc;	 And when it is healed, put on the natural balm of althea and oil, as we have said, then instruct them to move it a little at a time.
et quant tu avras ce fait, si la fai seoir sus I siege, et li comande k’elle se preigne;	 And when you have done this, make her sit on the seat, and tell her to take hold.
et la fai esternuer.	 And make her sneeze.
de ceste meisme maniere a tout la secondine	 De this same manner to all the secondine
Quant il vient fuer en ceste maniere a tout la secondine, si cope la secondine a ton ungle, tant que li moistors soit vuidie;	 When it comes out this way with all the snot, cut the mucus with your fingernail until the moisture is emptied.
et se li enfes pent sus sa faice et sus son col, si la cope des la boude, qu’elle ne soit retenue, et muere li enfes;	 And if the child vomits on its face and neck, cut it off from the mouth so that it is not retained, and let the child die.
puis boute l’enfant dedens, tant que tu l’aies mis si com il covient, et comande a la femme qu’elle se preigne aucune fois:	 Then push the child inside, until you have placed it as needed, and instruct the woman to take some time.
adonques si istra legierement.	 Then withdraw lightly.
de l’issue des gemelz	 of the birth of twins
Saiches que gemeil naissent maintes fois, et aucune fois en naissent III ou IIII;	 Know that twins are often born, and sometimes three or four at once;
et ceu n’est mie estrainge chose, et poc avient.	 And this is not an unusual thing, nor does it happen often.
Dui sont estrainge chose, et ne vivent mie, se poc nom;	 Two are strange things, and do not live, if at all;
je sai ceu, qu’il soient multipliiet, et sont desevrez par lou syfac qui les devise, qui est liiez a la boude;	 I know these, that they are multiple, and are divided by the umbilical cord that surrounds them, which is tied to the womb;
et aucune fois issent ausi naturelment com uns tous sous, si com nos avons dit.	 And sometimes they come out as naturally as one alone, as we have said.
Et s’il issent griement, si la cure si com nos avons dit, et soit li baile subtilz, et faice tost et legierement ceu qu’elle fait;	 And if they come out violently, then treat it as we have said, and let the midwife be skilled, and act quickly and lightly as she knows how.
et faice ensi com il vaut mues a salut.	 And make sure to do so in such a way as to promote healing.
de plusors enfans	 of many children
Aucune fois sont formez en la marris I ou II ou III ou IIII ou V ou VI ou VII, ou plusors jusc’a XV, et sont tout formeit en forme d’enfant par le mesurement dou saige glorious, et couvient que li baile saiche tout ceu, car par aventure semblans chose li avient;	 Sometimes they are formed in the womb one or two or three or four or five or six or seven, and even more up to fifteen, and all are formed in the shape of a child by the measuring of the wise Glorious One, and it is necessary that the midwife knows all this, for perhaps similar things may happen;
si faice selonc ceu qu’il covient.	 do so accordingly.
de l’enfant mort	 of the dead child
Quant tu cures la femme de l’enfant mort ou ventre, si com j’ai dit en la division, et il ne vient fuers, et tu es constrains d’ovraige de mains;	 When you care for a woman who has had a stillbirth or miscarriage, as I have said in the division, and it does not come out, and you are forced to work with your hands;
si covient que tu saiches se li femme est de saine vertut, et n’ait accident ou elle ait paor de mort;	 then you must know if the woman is of sound health, and has no complications or fear of death;
si covient que li femme soit sovinee sus son dos, et soit ses chiés enclins aval, et les jambes levees;	 If necessary, let the woman be placed on her back, and her head inclined downwards, and her legs raised.
et li ministre la teigne de II pars, ou elle soit liie au lit si qu’elle ne soit traite au dessendement de l’enfant;	 And let the midwife apply the scissors in two parts, so that she is tied to the bed and not moved during the birth of the child.
puis frotez la bouche de la marris d’oiles moistes avec muscillaige de altee et de fenugrec et semence de lin, puis oigne li baile ses mains de ces oiles et de ces muscillaiges;	 Then rub the mouth of the mother with moist oil, mixed with a paste of althea and fenugreek and flax seed, then let the midwife anoint her hands with these oils and pastes.
puis les boute en la marris legierement, puis quiere I leu ou elle boute les oncines que soient covenaubles a ceu, et pren warde se li enfes est apparilliez qu’il dessende sus son chief;	 Then gently insert them into the mother, then seek out the place where she inserted the ointments, and take care to see if the child is prepared to descend onto its head.
si fiche les oncines en ses eulz ou en son col ou en sa bouche ou en som palais ou desoz la barbe ou en la forcele ou pres des costez, et se li dessendemens est sus piez, se li fiche ou poignil et as costes moienes;	 If the ointments are inserted into his eyes or neck or mouth or palate or under the chin or in the armpits or near the ribs, and if the descent is onto the feet, then insert it into the big toe and in the middle of the ribs.
et covient qu’il teigne l’oncine a sa main destre, et mette la corbeure entre ses dois de la senestre main, et li boute a tout sa main legierement, et fiche l’oncine en aucun de ces leus que nos avons dit, tant qu’il viegne a la chose vuide;	 And it is necessary that he holds the awl in his right hand, and places the handle between his fingers of the left hand, and pushes with all his hand lightly, and drives the awl into one of these places that we have said, until it reaches the empty space;
et c’est li forme de l’oncine:	 And this is the shape of the awl:
puis fiche encontre I autre oncine, ou le tier se tu en as mestier, si que li estractions soit igalz;	 Then drive against the other awl, or the third if you need it, so that the extraction is equal.
et puis l’estent igalment en movant d’une part et d’autre, por mues issir, et soit li oncines dentez por mues tenir, si com ci est li forme:	 And then they are equally extended by moving from one side to the other, so that it comes out easily, and the awls should be toothed to hold well, as shown in this figure:
Et s’il en demoure une partie, si oigne li baile aucuns de ses dois d’oile, et les boute en celle partie, et traie l’autre partie;	 And if a part remains, then anoint the wound with some oil from his fingers, and push it into that part, and pull out the other part;
et s’il en i demoure point, si met cest oncine ou plus haut leu, et fai ceu tant qu’il s’en isse tout fuers.	 And if any remains behind, then place this ointment in a higher place, and do this until it all comes out.
Et se l’une mains vient devant l’autre, et il ne puet ramener por l’estreignement, si covient que tu envoloupes sus I drapeil, tant qu’il isse tote;	 And if one hand comes before the other and cannot be returned due to tightness, then you must wrap it in a cloth until it all comes out.
puis la cope en la jointure de la plante ou au coute, et ensi covient que tu faices en l’autre main, et as II piés.	 Then cut in the joint of the foot or with the heel, and thus you must do with the other hand and both feet.
Et se li chiés de l’enfant est gros et il est estrois en l’issue, ou il ait ou chief aigue assemblee, si covient que tu boute le spatumile espinous entre tes dois, et fent le chief et estrai l’aigue;	 And if the child's head is large and it is tight at the outlet, or if there is sharp water collected at the head, then you must put a thorny spatula between your fingers, pierce the head and draw out the water.
ou tu la ront a l’estrument qui est apelez «almidach», de coi li forme vient avec les estrumens ou chapistre qui est aprés cestui;	 Or take to the instrument that is called "almidach," from which the form comes with the instruments in the following chapter.
et ensi meisme faice se li enfes a grant chief naturelment;	 And do the same if the child has a large head naturally;
et puis traie fuer les osses as tenailles, et se li chiés saut fuer et il estraint a la forcele, si soit fendus, tant que li moistors qui est ou pis issue fuer;	 And then draw out the bones with tweezers, and if the head jumps out and is stuck in the forceps, it should be cut open until the moisture that is in the worst part comes out.
et s’elle ne puet issir, si le cope par pieces au mues que tu pues;	 And if it cannot come out, then cut it into pieces as best you can;
et s’il est enflez au ventre ou desoz les costez, si covient que tu lou perces tant que li moistors corre.	 And if it is swollen in the belly or under the ribs, then you must puncture until the moisture runs out.
Et se li enfes est sus ses piez, si est li attraction legiere, et li adrecemens a la bouche de la marris est legier.	 And if the child is standing on its feet, then the pulling is gentle, and the placement at the mother's breast is easy.
Et s’il est estrois au ventre ou au pis, si couvient que tu l’estraies a I drapeil envoloupeit sus la main;	 And if it is narrow in the belly or in the chest, then you must extract it with a cloth wrapped around your hand.
et fent le ventre ou le pis, tant que li moistors qui i est corre;	 And if it punctures the belly or the breast, until the moisture within is corrected.
et se li autre membre sont osteit, et li chiez demoure, si boute li baile sa main em parfont de la marris, et le traie jusc’a la bouche de la marris;	 And if other members are removed and the head remains, then the healer should insert his hand into the depth of the wound and draw it out to the mouth of the wound.
puis i boute I oncine ou II, et le trai fuer;	 Then he places one or two fingers in and draws it strongly.
et se li bouche de la marris est retrecie por aposteme chaut qui i est venus, si n’i covient mie travillier, ains covient amenistrer choses moistes et grasses;	 And if the mouth of the wound is narrowed due to a hot abscess that has formed there, it is not necessary to work on it, but rather one should apply moist and fatty substances.
et li amenistre emplaustres, et siece en aigue mollifians et amoistans.	 And the healer applies poultices, soaking them in softening and moistening water.
Et se li enfes est sus son costeit, et tu le pues mettre igal, si amenistre ceu que nos avons dit en l’enfant vif;	 And if the child is on its side, and you can turn it over, then treat it as we have said for a living child.
et s’on nen ait pooir, si lou trai fuer par pieces, et n’i laissier rien de la secondine.	 And if one cannot do it, then draw it out piece by piece, and leave nothing of the arrowhead.
Et quant tu avras ce fait, se li amenistre ceu que nos avons dit ens apostemes chaus que vienent en la marris;	 And when you have done this, if it happens that what we have said comes to pass in abscesses like those which come on the thighs;
et se decorremens de sanc vient, si soit mise en aigue restraignant, et li amenistre autres cures.	 and if bleeding occurs, place it in boiling water to stop the flow, and apply other treatments.
Et je vis une femme en cui ventre uns enfes avoit esteit mors, puis consut I autre sus celui, et refut mors li autres.	 And I saw a woman whose womb an infant had died in, and then another was conceived above it, and that one also died.
Aprés lonc tens li vint uns apostemes en la boude, et enfla tant qu’il ovrit, et comensa a grant porreture.	 After a long time, she developed an abscess in the breast, which swelled until it burst, and began to discharge greatly.
je fui apelez a la cure, et i pensai lonc tens, et ne pot soder li plaie.	 I was called to treat it, and thought long about it, but the wound could not heal.
Je mis sus emplaustre de fort attraction, et en issit uns os, et aprés aucuns jors uns autres.	 I placed a strong drawing plaster on it, and from it came out a bone, and after some days another one.
Je me mervillai mout, por ceu c’ou ventre n’a point d’os.	 I was very astonished by this, for there are no bones in the belly.
Si pensai que c’estoit des os d’un enfant mort.	 So I thought that these were the bones of a dead child.
Je quis la plaie, et en traï mains os, tant que li femme fut em millor point;	 I saw the wound, and drew many bones from it until the woman was in a better state;
et vesquit li femme lonc tens ensi, et issoit adés un poc de bowe dou leu;	 and the woman lived for a long time thus, and a little pus always came out of the place.
et je n’ai recordeit cest chapistre fuer que por ceu que, quant li maistres trueve une estrainge chose, qu’il i saiche mettre aide.	 and I have not written this chapter except because when the master finds something strange, he should know how to provide help.
dou ramener la marris a son leu	 To return the limb to its place
Ci aprés vient li forme dou pressor, a coi on ewe les livres;	 Here follows the form of the press, for which we use the books;
et a II tornans as II chiés des II liiens.	 and at two turns are two keys of two locks.
Toutevoie, li cornes soit plus subtilz dou restrictoire, et soit fais de ebene ou de bux;	 However, the horns should be more subtle in the restrictor, and should be made of boxwood or ebony;
et soit li bouche dou fust I doi de large, et li marge des arbres I doit, et de lonc une palme et demi;	 and the mouth of the wood should be two fingers wide, and the margin of the tree one finger, and in length a palm and a half;
et enmi les II liemens soient dui ajostemens de cest meisme fust, qui soient fermeit en l’un et en l’autre, de demi palme de lonc ou un poc plus;	 and between the two locks there should be two supports of this same wood, which are fixed in one and the other, half a palm long or slightly more;
et cist dui ajostement sont bouteit en la bouche de la marris por ovrir quant on torne les II cornes.	 and these two supports are fitted into the mouth of the matrix to open when one turns the two horns.
Une autre forme, a sa semblance plus subtilz et plus legiere, soit faite de fust de ebene ou de bux, selonc la semblance des tenailles;	 Another form, more subtle and lighter, should be made from boxwood or ebony, according to the shape of the pincers;
et ait as II chiés II ajostemens, si com tu vois, d’une palme de lonc, et II dois de large;	 And it should have two heads and two settings, as you see, one palm in length, and two fingers in width.
et quant tu vues ovrir la marris a tout l’estrument, si fai seoir la femme sor I lit, les piez pendant et les jambes overtes, puis boute les II ajostemens ajostez ensamble en la marris, et tien le chief de l’estrument desoz entre ses cuixes;	 And when you see the instrument open completely, let the woman sit on the bed with her feet hanging and her legs spread apart, then insert the two settings closely together into the vagina, and hold the head of the instrument underneath between her thighs.
puis oevre ta main a tout l’estrument, si com tu as fait as tenailles igalment, selonc la quantiteit que tu vues ovrir la bouche de la marris, tant que li baile faice ceu qu’elle vuet.	 Then work your hand on the entire instrument in the same way you did with the pincers, according to the quantity by which you see opening the mouth of the vagina, until the patient does what she wants.
Cist estrument sont tuit sormontez, et sont multiplies lor semblances;	 This instrument is all surpassed, and their likenesses are multiplied.
et quant li mires les ait apareilliez, tant est plus hastans li oevre, et plus haute as homes por lor quantiteit.	 And when the mirror has prepared them, so much the more hurried is the work, and higher for men by their quantity.
Si ne despire mie l’estrument que tu ne l’aies apparelliet, car lor necessitez n’est mie escusauble.	 Do not despise the instrument before you have prepared it, for its necessity is inexcusable.
Quant li secondine est retenue a l’enfantement, si covient que tu comandes a la malaide qu’ele reteigne son alaine, et puis la fai esternuer de condisi, et li estraint tes mains a la bouche et au neis;	 When the secondine is retained during childbirth, you must instruct the patient to hold her breath, then make her sneeze by condiment, and hold your hands to her mouth and nose.
et s’elle saut per ceu, bien est.	 And if she dies from this, it is good.
Se ceu non, si prent I pot, et fai I pertus ou cuvercle, et i met herbes que puissent ovrir la bouche de la marris, si com calament, rue, anis, camomille, cassialigne et centoire;	 If not, then take a pot and make a hole in the lid, and put in it herbs that can open the woman's mouth, such as calamint, rue, anise, chamomile, cassia and centaury;
toutes ces herbes, ou aucunes d’eles, soient cuites ou pot en aigue sus le feu;	 All these herbs, or some of them, should be cooked in water over the fire.
puis met une caine ou pertus dou pot, et l’autre chief en la bouche de la marris, et la teigne tant que li vapors viegne dedens la marris;	 Then put a tube or hole from the pot, and the other end in the mouth of the patient, and hold it until the steam enters the mouth.
puis la fai esternuer, si com nos avons dit.	 Then make them sneeze, as we have said.
Si saut li secondine hastanment.	 Si la seconde fois hâte-toi.
Et s’elle remaint aprés ceste cure, et n’ist mie fuer, si comande a la baile qu’ele moille sa main senestre en oile de sesement ou en muscillaige de altee, et puis la boute en la nature, et quiere la secondine;	 And if she remains after this treatment, and is not cured, as we have said. Command the nurse to moisten her left hand in oil of sweet almonds or musk-scented oil of althea, then insert it into the vagina, and seek the second uterus;
et quant elle l’avra trovee, si la preigne et l’estende poc et poc droitement, si que li marris ne chiece a l’estraction;	 and when she has found it, take hold of it and draw it out little by little straightly, so that the patient does not feel pain at the extraction.
mais la covient movoir legierement a destre et a senestre, et puis traie;	 but you must move it gently to the right and to the left, then pull.
si venra et se desaerdra.	 it will come out and dislocate again.
Et se li bouche de la marris est jai estrecie, nos avons dit la cure d’esternuer, et de fumigation des herbes;	 And if the mouth of the nose is narrowly constricted, we have said the cure of sneezing, and of fumigation with herbs;
et s’elle n’ist de tout ceu que nos avons dit, si garde que tu ne foloies au traire;	 and if it does not come out from all that we have said, beware that you do not pull too hard;
mais il couvient que ceu qui est a la bouche de la marris, que tu le lies a la cuixe de la femme, puis la clisterize d’oignement tetrafarmaçon;	 but it is necessary that what is at the mouth of the nose, you tie it to the thigh of the woman, then give her an enema with four-leaf medicine.
si la porrira et remettra, et venra fuer;	 so she will vomit and expel it, and then fart.
mais toutevoie, quant elle porrist si en vient male odor au stomac et au chief, et blece la malaide.	 but nonetheless, when she farts, a bad smell comes to the stomach and head, and harms the patient.
Si covient donques fumigations covenaubles a ceu:	 If it is therefore necessary, appropriate fumigations are required for this purpose:
aucun des anciens ont esproveit fumigation de cresson et de figues seches.	 any of the ancients have proven fumigation with fresh watercress and dried figs.
Li forme de l’estrument a coi on fumige la femme a la retenue des flors et de la secondine si est ceste:	 The shape of the instrument used to fumigate the woman for retaining the menses and the afterbirth is as follows:
Et est de voirre semblant a une caine, et met on le chief subtil en la nature, et les chiés larges sus le feu;	 And it is like a reed, and one places the subtle end into the body, and the wide ends over the fire;
et soit li fumigations sus les charbons, et la teigne tant qu’elle soit gastee, et rencomence une autre.	 and let the fumigation be on the charcoal, and continue until it is completely burned out, then repeat with another one.
de percier lou fondement	 To pierce the anus
Maint enfant naissent qui n’ont mie le fondement perciet, ains l’ait estoupeit uns subtilz syfac:	 Many children are born whose fundament is not yet pierced, but rather closed by a thin membrane:
si covient donques a la baile qu’ele perce celui syfac a son doit, et ne lou perce mie de spatumile agut, et garse le lacement qu’elle ne le touche;	 therefore it is necessary for the midwife to pierce that membrane with her finger, and do not pierce it with a sharp stick, and take care that she does not touch it with pus; ︎
puis met sus lainne moillie en vin et en oile, puis la cure d’oignement tant qu’il soit sanez.	 then place on it a wet cloth soaked in wine and oil, then continue the treatment of poultices until he is cured.
Et se tu doutes qu’il ne restoupe, si met ou pertus une caine de plonc, et li laisse mains jors, et soit ostee quant li enfes vuet aler en chambres.	 Et si vous avez des doutes qu'il ne guérira pas, alors insérez dans l'ouverture un morceau de plomb, et laissez-le en place pendant moins de jours, et retirez-le lorsque l'enfant veut aller aux toilettes.
Et aucune fois vient cist estoupemens de soudement de plaie ou d’aposteme;	 And sometimes this swelling comes suddenly from a wound or an abscess;
si covient coper celui soudement:	 then it is necessary to cover that sudden (swelling) immediately:
si soit curez, si com nos avons dit de la caine de plonc.	 if it is healed, just as we have said of the linen of lead.
de la fistule dou fondement	 of the rectal fistula
Fistules qui vienent desoz le fondement sont nodation, et groissor que vienent delez lou fondement defuer, ou en l’espaice des II parties, si a une fistule ou plusors;	 Fistulas that come from under the anus are knots, and those that come beside the anus outward, or in the space of the two parts, if there is one fistula or several; ‌
et quant celle nodation est anciene, si aoeuvre, et encort moistor awouse blainche ou subtilz bowe, et aucune fois sont ces fistule persans;	 and when that knot is old, it works, and causes more moisture, which is white or subtle pus, and sometimes these fistulas are persistent;
et sont conues par ceu qu’il en ist ou egestion ou ventositeit quant li malaide fait egestion, et par aventure en saut uns vers.	 And they are known by this: that it comes out in egestion or ventosity when the patient passes waste, and sometimes one jumps out.
Et si a fistules que percent jusc’a la vessie, et jusc’a la moitiet de la verge;	 And there are fistulas that go all the way to the bladder, and halfway down the penis;
et parvienent jusc’a la jointure de la cuixe, et jusc’a nout de la kowe.	 and reach as far as the junction of the thigh, and even to the tip of the scrotum.
Et ensi conoist on la fistule persant au fondement, et ne mie persant:	 And thus one knows if a fistula is present at the anus, or not present:
et est que tu boutes ton doi indice ou fondement, et boute une aguille subtil d’arain ou de fer en la fistule quant il n’i a tortuositeit.	 and it is that you put your index finger into the anus, and insert a fine needle of brass or iron into the fistula when there is no tortuosity.
Et s’il ait tortuositeit, si i boute une tente de plonc subtil, ou I poil de cheval, tant que tu sentes la tente ou le poil a ton doit;	 And if there is tortuosity, then insert a fine lead tent or a horse hair into it, until you feel the tent or hair with your finger;
et se tu ne le sens, et il ne vient dou pertus egestion ne ventositeit ne ver, si com nos avons dit:	 And if you do not feel it, and neither excrement nor flatulence nor feces come out of the anus, as we have said:
saiches qu’elle ne perce mie;	 know that it does not burst;
si te haste dou curer.	 if you hasten with the cure.
Et quant li fistule est persans jusc’a la vessie ou jusc’a conduit de l’urine, si en saut li urine, et ne puet soudeir par medicines.	 And when the fistula reaches the bladder or the passage of urine, then urine leaks out, and it cannot be healed by medicines.
S’elle est percie jusc’a la jointure de la cuixe, si est li tente venans jusc’au leu;	 If it is pierced up to the hip joint, then the tentacle comes to the place;
s’il n’i a tortuositeit et li invention de la dolor entor, si est qu’il en ist adés bowe, et n’i vaut medicine ne soudement par oignement;	 if there is no twisting and the pain spreads around, it is likely that it will come out immediately, and neither medicine nor a sudden poultice will be of any use;
et en ces fistules persans n’a point de cure fuer que labor, et vaniteit des folz mires qui s’en entremettent.	 And in these Persian fistulas, there is no cure except labor, and the vanity of foolish doctors who meddle with them.
En celle qui n’est mie persans et n’est mie anciene, a esperance de saniteit par fer, si com j’ai esproveit, et est que li malaides gise entre tes mains sus son dos;	 In those that are not Persian and not very old, there is hope of health through iron, as I have experienced, and it is for the patient to lie on his back between your hands;
et li lieve les jambes jusque sus ses cuixes, et ait ses cuixes enclinees a son ventre;	 And he raises his legs up to his hips, and let his hips be inclined towards his belly;
puis boute une tente d’arain, ou de plonc s’il i a tortuositeit, tant que tu saiches ou li tente vient.	 then put an iron tent, or of lead if there is crookedness, so that you know where the tent comes.
Se li malaides la sent entor le fondement, si covient que tu i boutes ton doi indice, se sens adonques que li tente l’ait perciet;	 If the patient feels it around the anus, then you must put your index finger there, if you then feel that the tent has pierced;
et soit descoverte ou tu sens entre ton doit le syfac ou la char, adonques saiches qu’elle est persans;	 and let it be uncovered where you feel between your finger the pus or flesh, then know that it is perforated;
si n’i travillier mie c’on ne la puet saner.	 do not tamper with it if it cannot be healed.
On dist toutevoie c’on em puet bien saner aucuns, mais ce avient poc;	 However, one can indeed heal some [cases], but this happens rarely;
et li aide c’on i fait, si est c’on eschaufe le cautere subtil selonc la largesce de la fistule, si com il est devant dit;	 and the aid consists in heating the subtle cautery according to the width of the fistula, as has been said before;
et le boute tout chaut en la fistule, tant qu’il viegne delez le fondement;	 And he pours all hot into the fistula, until it reaches near the anus.
et faice ceu II fois ou III, tant que tu saiches que ces chars fautrees soient arses, qui sont semblant a une penne d’oiseil;	 And do this two or three times, until you know that these warty growths are burned, which resemble a bird’s feather.
et puis le cure de tentes moillies em burre, tant que celle chars isse fuer, puis le cure d’oignement enjanrant char et soudant.	 And then treat it with moistened bandages soaked in butter, until those warts come out, and then treat with a salve to prevent inflammation and heal.
S’il est ensi sanez, c’est bien.	 If he is thus treated, this is good.
Se ceu, nom autrement ne puet estre sanez;	 If this cannot be cured otherwise;
et se li tente entre, et ne perce jusc’au doit qui est ou fondement, et a entre ton doi et la tente une coverture espesse de char ou de syfac, et tu vois la fistule a ceu qui enseut la coverture dou keur;	 and if the abscess enters and does not perforate as far as the bone in the anus, and there is a thick covering of flesh or pus between your finger and the abscess, and you see the fistula at that place where the covering joins.
si le cope des l’encomencement de la fistule, et boute adés avant la tente, et pues le cautere aprés, tant qu’il viegne au chief de la tente;	 si la cautérisation commence dès le début de la fistule,
et sera delivré li tente, et cherra;	 et puis cautérise ensuite,
puis mondefie celles chars fautrees que semblent une penne d’oisel, et n’en remaigne niant.	 and there will be no trace remaining.
Et si li sans te vaint, et cort entre toi et l’uevre, si le cauterize de feu ou de medicine ague.	 And if the pus overcomes you and cuts between you and the work, then cauterize it with fire or medicinal vinegar.
Car li cauteres de feu assemble II bones choses:	 il chasse la maladie qui est dedenz, et fait cicatriser le plaie de dehors.
c’est a savoir, l’arsure de ces chars ajostees, et l’esteinchement de sanc et la sechor de la moistor;	 et li cauteres de feu fait tant qu’il n’i puet durer ne remedier.
puis le cure de tentes moillies em burre ou en choz broiez, tant que li leus giete bowe, et isse fuer li chars arse en la bowe;	 et sachez que nule autre cose ne poez aider fors le cautere de feu.
puis cure la plaie des oignemens soudans enjanrans dure char, et sont les medicines seches.	 Et sachies que li cauteres de feu est plusors foys nesces en ceste maistrie.
Car quant il est restoree, si est sanee et ne revient mie.	 For when it is restored, it is healed and does not return.
Et se fistule vient jusc’a parfont dou fondement, et est esloigniez dou cors, se li boute ton doi ou fondement, et enquier ceu.	 And if the fistula reaches as far as the anus, and is distant from the body, then you should pour oil or wine into the anus, and inquire about this.
Se tu sens la tente, et entre II est li toile ou li syfac ou chars, ou il est pres a percier, si n’i ait fuers que voie de fiance et d’esperance, par l’aministrement de l’une des III manieres:	 If you feel the tent, and there are two fabrics or cloths or tents within it, which is about to tear, then let there be no one inside except for those who are trustworthy and hopeful, by means of one of the three methods:
ou tu le cauterizes si com nos avons dit, ou tu le cope jusc’a fons, ou se tu pues si i met tentes et cure si com premier;	 Or you cauterize it as we have said, or you cut to the bottom, or if you can, place tents there and treat as before;
et n’aler mie trop em parfont, que tu ne coper le tenement qui tient le fondement, et viegne li egestions par lai sens volenteit;	 And do not go too deep, lest you cut the foundation that holds the bottom, and the evacuation comes out involuntarily;
puis le cure, si com nos avons dit;	 Then treat it as we have said;
par aventure si sera sanez, ou tu esloigne celle coverture et la munde puis qu’elle est copee delez lou fondement, ou par tente ou par autre estrument apointé;	 Perhaps it will be healed, or you remove that covering and clean it after it has been cut near the bottom, either by tent or by another suitable instrument.
puis mondefie cele char fautree qui est en la plaie, tant com tu pues;	 Then cleanse the wound with a poultice as best you can;
puis estudie a restorer la plaie, et a demorer la fistule en la partie defuers le fondement:	 then study to restore the wound, and to stop the fistula in the area below the anus:
si iert plus legiere chose au malaide.	 this would be easier for the patient.
Et aucune fois sont fistules selonc ceste maniere:	 And sometimes fistulas are like this:
et est quant tu boutes la tente en la fistule, et elle est ou costeit dou fondement delez lou cuir desus, si pren une tente percie au chief selonc ceste forme:	 and it is when you insert the tent into the fistula, which is near the edge of the anus on the skin above, then take a pointed tent according to this form:
Et i boute I fil tort en II, et boute la tente a tout le fil en la fistule tant qu’il soit au chief.	 And you push a twisted thread into it, and push the tent along with all of the thread into the fistula until it reaches the top.
S’elle est persans en la marge dou fondement dedens, adonc estrai lou fil de celui pertus, ensi que tu boutes ton doi ou fondement;	 If it is passing through the margin of the anus inside, then draw out the thread from that hole, so that you insert your finger into the anus;
et trai le chief dou fil, et assemble les II chiés ensamble, et estraint l’un a l’autre, et le laisse I jor ou II;	 and pull out the end of the thread, and tie the two ends together, and hold them firmly against each other, and leave it for one or two days;
et le restraint aucune fois, tant que li filz cope ces chars que sont entre dous, et chiecent;	 And sometimes it restricts, so much so that the son cuts those carts that are between two, and they fall.
puis cure la plaie tant qu’elle soit soudee et sanee.	 then heal the wound until it is healed and healthy.
Se li fistule ne perce, si la fai percier en toutes les manieres que tu pues, s’ele n’est trop em parfont.	 If the fistula does not burst, then make it burst in all ways that you can, unless it is too deeply embedded.
Car il ne covient mie faire por le lacement coper si em parfont, et puis le cure, si com nos avons dit, tant qu’il soit sanez.	 For it is not necessary to cover the ulcer with a cap so deeply, and then treat it as we have said, until it is healed.
Li forme dou spatumile espinous dont on fent la fistule si est mout agus d’une, part et trenchans;	 The shape of the spine-like stylus used to make a fistula is very sharp at one end and cutting;
et d’autre part non, por ceu c’on ne cope mie ceu c’on ne doit mie copeir, si com tu vois ci:	 and on the other side no, so that you do not cut what should not be cut, as you can see here:
des emorroydes	 hemorrhoids
Emorrydes sont selonc II manieres:	 There are two types of emollients:
ou elles sont dedens le fondement, ausi com grain de resin, et s’en i a petites et grans, et en cort adés sanc, et s’en i a une ou plusors, et sont defuer le fondement et au chief dou fondement;	 or they are inside the rectum, like resin grains, and there can be small and large ones, and blood always flows from them, and there is one or several of them, and they are outside the rectum and at the opening of the rectum;
mais celles qui sont defuer si ont poc de moistor, et encort adés ou un poc d’aigue citrine ou un poc de sanc, et ont la color dou cors;	 But those which lack moisture have little of it, and sometimes a little yellow water or blood, and they retain the body's color.
et li cure de ces qui les ont dedens le fondement, si est que tu comandes au malaide qu’il s’espreigne por aleir en chambres, tant que li fondemens li isse fuer, et c’aperent li filz;	 And the treatment for those who have them in the anus is to instruct the patient to sprinkle on himself so that he may go into rooms until the anus releases them, and the threads appear.
si te haste, et le pent as tenailles, ou tu le tien a ton ungle, puis le cope en ses racines;	 If you hurry, and you grasp it with pincers, or hold it with your nail, then cut it at its roots;
et se li uncine ne les pueent tenir por ses moistors, si les prent a I drapeil, ou a couton, ou d’une piece de chamelot;	 And if the tweezers cannot hold them due to their moisture, then take them with a cloth or thread, or a piece of camlet.
et les estrai a tes dois, puis les cope, et poudre desus aucunes chaudes poudres que soient en leu de cautere;	 And pull them with your fingers, then cut them, and sprinkle some hot powders that are suitable for cauterization on top.
ou tu les cauterize si com il est dit ou chapistre de cautere, pues les cure d’autres cures tant qu’il soit sanez;	 When you cauterize them as it is said in the chapter on cautery, then proceed with other treatments until he is healed.
et se li fondemens ne puet issir, si clisterize le malaide de clistere mordant et aspre por laver ceu qui est ou fondement, si qu’il puist issir apertement;	 And if the foundation cannot come out, then enema the patient with a biting and harsh enema to clean what is in the foundation, so that it may come out freely.
cant li malaides se preint, et se li fil sont fuer dou fondement, si est li cure legiere;	 When the patient has hemorrhoids and if the threads are protruding from the foundation, then the treatment is light.
et est que tu les preignes a ton ungle ou as tenailles, et les cope, puis les cure si com nos avons dit, tant qu’il soit sanez, et qu’il redoute l’incision par fer.	 And do this: you take them with your nail or tweezers, and cut them, then treat them as we have said, until he is healed, and that he fears the incision by iron.
Si covient que tu amenistre la costure selonc ceste maniere:	 So it is necessary that you make the suture in this manner:
pren I fil tort, et le boute en une aguille, et puis trai le fil au desus et fai percier l’aguille d’autre part, et torne les II chiez dou fil desoz l’aguille, et si soit dou large;	 Grasp the thread twisted, and put it in a needle, then pull the thread on top and make the needle pierce from the other side, and turn the two ends of the thread under the needle, and let it be wide.
et estraint le fil forment, puis noe le fil, et estrai l’aguille, et fai ensi de toz les autres, et en laisse I por corre la superfluiteit dou sanc;	 And strain the thread strongly, then tie a knot in the thread, and pull out the needle, and do thus with all the others, and leave one for running the superfluity of blood.
puis met sus le fondement I drapeil moilliet en oile roset ou en cerote, et met sus le fondement, et comande au malaide k’il repose;	 Then put on a bandage soaked in rose oil or wax, and put it on the wound, and instruct the patient to rest.
et puis le laisse tant qu’il chiecent, et quant il seront cheut, si les cure d’oignement et d’autre cure, tant qu’il soit sanez.	 And then leave them until they become suppurating, and when they have fallen out, then treat them with salve and other treatments, until they are healed.
dou sechement dou fiens ou fondement	 Of dryness of the intestines in the lower body
Maintes fois avient sechement de fiens en l’intestine, et par constrignement de nature, et quant li maladie est vielle et medicine n’i vaut.	 It often happens that there is dryness of the intestines in the bowels, due to natural constraint, and when the illness is old and medication does not help.
Si covient que tu reses a la point d’un spatumile ou a ton ungle l’escorce desus, qui ne le laisse a moistir;	 If it is necessary for you to remove the scab with the tip of a spatula or your nail on top, do not allow it to moisten.
puis le cure tant qu’il soit sodez si com il covient;	 then heal it until it is dry as it should be;
et s’il ne puet soder, si rencomence la rasure plus fort que devant, tant qu’il saine mout, et soit escorchiez;	 and if it cannot dry out, then repeat the scraping more strongly than before, so that it heals well and is peeled off.
puis le cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	 then heal it until it is healed.
dou fremit	 from shivering
Formice est une petite apparance fautree antor le cors, et va mout em parfont;	 Formica is a small appearance of hair under the skin, and it goes very deep into the body;
et aucune fois la trueve li frois, et le sent on ausi comme mort de fremit, et vient en tout le cors, et plus as mains que autre part.	 and sometimes the cold finds it, and one feels it as if dead with trembling, and it spreads throughout the body, and more in the hands than anywhere else.
Et li cure si est que tu pren une cainne d’une penne d’oie, ou une penne de vultul fort, et met celle caine sus le fremit, tant que li cercles porpreigne le fremit tot entor;	 And the treatment is such that you take a quill from a goose feather, or a strong quill from an ox, and place that quill on the trembling, so that the circle around the trembling turns purple all around.
puis torne ta main a tout la cainne tant que tu copes tout entor le fremit, et le met em parfont, et esraiche le fremit de ses racines.	 Then turn your hand to the whole chain so that you cut all around the freckle, and put it in completely, and eradicate the freckle from its roots.
Et se tu vues, si fai ceu d’une caine d’arain ou de fer selonc ceste forme, et soit subtilz desoz et traians desus:	 And if you see this, do it with a reed of bronze or iron in the same way, and let it be thin below and pointed above.
ne mie perciet, por mues tenir au doi, et mues presser.	 Do not pierce, but instead hold to the two (sides), and press firmly.
Et se tu vues, si cauterize lou fremit, si com il est devant ou chapistre de cautere.	 And if you see it, then cauterize the freckle as is described in the chapter on cautery.
de la forme dou clistere	 Of the form of the clyster
Aucune fois fait on clistere d’argent ou d’archaut, ou d’arain fondut ou mailliet;	 Sometimes one makes a cluster of silver or gold, or melted iron or brass;
et aucune fois fait on de ces estrumens petis et grans, selonc ces a cui il sont amenistrez.	 and sometimes one makes these instruments small or large, according to those for whom they are prepared.
Cil donques c’on amenistre en la cure des enfans et qui sont foible et dolorous, sont petis.	 Therefore, those that are prepared for the care of children who are weak and suffering should be small.
Li forme dou clistere petit et grant si est desus large, ou li ventres est liiez selonc ceste maniere:	 The form of the small or large clyster is thus wide at the top, where the stomach is tied in this manner:
et i ait une desevrance ou li ventres soit liiez, si com tu vois, et li chiez soit dedens perciez;	 And if there is an obstruction where the intestines are tied, as you see, and the head is pierced within;
et ait a l’un des costez II pertus, et en l’autre I;	 And let there be on one side two holes, and on the other side one hole.
et soit li ventres ou om met les medicines d’une vessie de beste ou de parchemin, et soit perciez tout entor de menus pertus, et ait entre chescun pertus I doit d’espaice, puis boute en ces pertus I fil fort de fil crut tort en X ou enqui entor, et assemble le ventre si com est une chievre;	 And let the belly, into which the medicines are placed, be of an animal's bladder or parchment, and let it be pierced all around with small holes, and between each hole there should be one finger's width, then insert into these holes a strong thread, twisted like a cross or around, and gather the belly together as if it were a goat;
et quant li medicine est dedens, si la lie a l’estrument devant d’un fil fort, puis clisterize;	 And when the medicine is inside, then bind it to the instrument in front with a strong thread, then perform an enema.
et c’est li forme dou cercle:	 And this is the shape of the circle:
Et soit li medicine ne trop chaude ne trop froide, et oint le chief dou clistere d’oile ou d’aubun d’uef, ou de semblant chose, puis le boute ens legierement;	 And let the medicine not be too hot or too cold, and anoint the head of the enema with oil or egg yolk, or a similar substance, then gently insert it.
puis l’espreigne li ministres a ses II mains ensamble, tant qu’il soit toz vuis, puis estrai lou clistere, et lieve li malaides ses jambes a la paroit, et se li medicine vuet issir, si la teigne tant com il puet;	 Then the minister wrings his hands together until they are completely empty, then he inserts the clyster, and lifts the patient's legs against the wall, and if the medicine wants to come out, then he holds it as long as he can.
et s’il dort une nuit atot, si est plus grans aide.	 And if he sleeps through the night, then there is even greater aid.
Et se tu le clisterizes em maladie de decorrement de ventre, et li medicine se haste d’issir, si le rencomence tant qu’il soit sanez.	 And if you enema him in the disease of diarrhea, and the medicine hastens to exit, then repeat it until he is cured.
Et se li emorroide sont ou fondement, ou aposteme, si soit li clistere ausi subtilz com por I enfant;	 And if the hemorrhoids are in the rectum or abscess, let the clyster be as thin as for a child;
et c’est li forme dou clistere subtil sus coi li cuir soit estraint:	 and this is the form of the subtle clyster with which the skin is drawn tight:
des plaies	 of wounds
Nos avons jai dit en la division la cure des plaies;	 We have already said in the section on the treatment of wounds;
or vos dirons les cures de mains et de medicine, selonc l’acomplissement.	 Or we will tell you about the treatments for hands and medicines, according to their completeness.
Je dis que les plaies sont diverses selonc ceu qu’elles sont faites, et selonc les leus ou les plaies sont faites, et de coi elles sont faites.	 I say that wounds are diverse according to what they are made of, and according to the places where the wounds are made, and by what they are made.
